{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_016L5ehwJC8CPr27SKmnTk17","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_014i1qYVWJL8GDBs6TA8zAPc","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/RELEASE_NOTES.md","content":"# Flipt Release Notes\n\n## Overview\n\nThis release focuses on improving OpenTelemetry (OTEL) tracing instrumentation in Flipt. The changes introduce better sampling control, distributed tracing propagator configuration, enhanced resource attributes, and support for OpenTelemetry Semantic Conventions for Feature Flags.\n\n## New Features\n\n### Tracing Configuration Enhancements\n\n#### **Sampling Ratio Control**\n- **Component**: [Tracing Configuration]\n- **Description**: Added `samplingRatio` configuration option to control the sampling rate of traces.\n- **Details**: The sampling ratio accepts a float value between 0 and 1 (inclusive), where:\n  - `0` = no traces are sampled (sampling disabled)\n  - `1` = all traces are sampled (no sampling)\n  - `0.1` = 10% of traces are sampled\n- **Configuration Example**:\n  ```yaml\n  tracing:\n    enabled: true\n    exporter: otlp\n    samplingRatio: 0.1  # Sample 10% of traces\n    otlp:\n      endpoint: localhost:4317\n  ```\n- **Default**: `1.0` (all traces sampled)\n- **API Reference**: Configuration is set via `flipt.schema.json` or YAML config files under `tracing.samplingRatio`\n\n#### **Multiple Propagator Support**\n- **Component**: [Tracing Configuration]\n- **Description**: Added support for configurable OpenTelemetry text map propagators to handle trace context propagation across services.\n- **Details**: Multiple propagators can be specified to support different distributed tracing standards. Supported options include:\n  - `tracecontext` — W3C Trace Context (default)\n  - `baggage` — W3C Baggage (default)\n  - `b3` — Zipkin B3 Single propagator\n  - `b3multi` — Zipkin B3 Multi propagator\n  - `jaeger` — Jaeger propagator\n  - `xray` — AWS X-Ray propagator\n  - `ottrace` — OT Trace propagator\n  - `none` — No propagation\n- **Configuration Example**:\n  ```yaml\n  tracing:\n    enabled: true\n    exporter: otlp\n    propagators:\n      - tracecontext\n      - baggage\n      - b3multi\n    otlp:\n      endpoint: localhost:4317\n  ```\n- **Default**: `[\"tracecontext\", \"baggage\"]`\n- **API Reference**: Configuration is set via `flipt.schema.json` or YAML config files under `tracing.propagators`\n\n### Enhanced Tracing Resource Attributes\n\n- **Component**: [OpenTelemetry Tracing]\n- **Description**: Improved the trace resource to include more comprehensive metadata about the Flipt service.\n- **Details**: The tracer provider now includes:\n  - Service name: `flipt`\n  - Service version: Flipt version\n  - Container information (if running in container)\n  - Host information (hostname, OS details)\n  - Process runtime information (Go version, runtime name)\n  - OTEL environment variables (automatic detection)\n  - Telemetry SDK information\n  - Schema URL for semantic convention compliance\n- **Impact**: Better trace correlation and service identification in distributed tracing backends\n\n### OpenTelemetry Semantic Conventions for Feature Flags\n\n- **Component**: [OTEL Attributes]\n- **Description**: Added support for OpenTelemetry's official semantic conventions for feature flags in span attributes.\n- **Details**: Trace spans now include standardized feature flag attributes:\n  - `ff.key` — The feature flag key (standardized attribute)\n  - `ff.provider_name` — The provider name set to \"Flipt\"\n  - `ff.variant` — The evaluated variant key (if applicable)\n  - Custom Flipt attributes:\n    - `flipt.flag` — Flag key\n    - `flipt.match` — Whether the flag matched\n    - `flipt.namespace` — Namespace key\n    - `flipt.flag_enabled` — Boolean flag enabled state\n    - `flipt.segment` — Segment key (deprecated)\n    - `flipt.segments` — List of matching segment keys\n    - `flipt.reason` — Evaluation reason\n    - `flipt.value` — Variant value\n    - `flipt.entity_id` — Entity ID\n    - `flipt.request_id` — Request ID\n- **Specification**: Follows [OpenTelemetry Feature Flags Semantic Conventions](https://opentelemetry.io/docs/specs/semconv/feature-flags/feature-flags-spans/)\n- **Impact**: Enables better trace analysis in observability platforms that support feature flag semantic conventions\n\n### OTEL Semantic Conventions Version Upgrade\n\n- **Component**: [OpenTelemetry Dependencies]\n- **Description**: Updated to the latest OpenTelemetry semantic conventions version (v1.24.0).\n- **Impact**: Access to latest semantic conventions and improved compatibility with modern observability backends\n\n## Configuration Examples\n\n### Basic OTLP Configuration with Sampling\n\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  samplingRatio: 0.5  # Sample 50% of traces\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: localhost:4317\n```\n\n### Advanced Configuration with Multiple Propagators\n\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  samplingRatio: 0.1\n  propagators:\n    - tracecontext\n    - baggage\n    - b3multi\n    - xray\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: otel-collector:4317\n    headers:\n      Authorization: Bearer your_token\n```\n\n### Jaeger Configuration with Sampling (Deprecated Exporter)\n\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: jaeger  # Deprecated - consider migrating to OTLP\n  samplingRatio: 1.0\n  jaeger:\n    host: localhost\n    port: 6831\n```\n\n### Zipkin Configuration with Propagators\n\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: zipkin\n  samplingRatio: 0.25\n  propagators:\n    - tracecontext\n    - baggage\n    - b3\n  zipkin:\n    endpoint: http://localhost:9411/api/v2/spans\n```\n\n## Deprecations\n\n### Jaeger Tracing Exporter (Existing Deprecation)\n\n- **Status**: Deprecated (as of v1.36.0)\n- **Details**: The Jaeger exporter is no longer actively maintained in OpenTelemetry. OpenTelemetry recommends using OTLP (OpenTelemetry Protocol) instead.\n- **Migration Path**:\n  1. Update your configuration to use `exporter: otlp`\n  2. Point to your Jaeger instance's OTLP receiver or use an OTLP-compatible backend\n  3. Test trace collection with the new configuration\n- **Timeline**: The Jaeger exporter will be removed in a future major version\n\n## Upgrade Guide\n\n### Step 1: Update Flipt\n\nUpdate to the latest version that includes these tracing improvements. The changes are backward compatible with existing configurations.\n\n### Step 2: Review Current Tracing Configuration (Optional)\n\nIf you are currently using tracing, check your existing configuration:\n\n```bash\n# Verify your current tracing configuration\ncat /path/to/your/flipt/config.yml | grep -A 20 \"^tracing:\"\n```\n\n### Step 3: Add Sampling Configuration (Recommended)\n\nTo optimize trace collection and reduce overhead, consider adding a sampling ratio:\n\n**Before:**\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: localhost:4317\n```\n\n**After:**\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  samplingRatio: 0.1  # Adjust based on your needs\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: localhost:4317\n```\n\n### Step 4: Configure Propagators (If Using Distributed Tracing)\n\nIf you're using distributed tracing with multiple services, specify propagators to match your infrastructure:\n\n**For W3C-compliant systems:**\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  propagators:\n    - tracecontext\n    - baggage\n```\n\n**For Zipkin-based systems:**\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  propagators:\n    - tracecontext\n    - baggage\n    - b3\n```\n\n**For AWS environments:**\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  propagators:\n    - tracecontext\n    - baggage\n    - xray\n```\n\n### Step 5: Validate Configuration\n\nTest your updated configuration:\n\n```bash\nflipt validate /path/to/your/flipt/config.yml\n```\n\nIf validation fails with propagator errors, check that all propagator names are valid (see list under \"Multiple Propagator Support\" above).\n\n### Step 6: Restart Flipt\n\nRestart your Flipt instance to apply the new configuration:\n\n```bash\n# Docker\ndocker restart flipt\n\n# Systemd\nsystemctl restart flipt\n\n# Manual\npkill flipt\n/path/to/flipt &\n```\n\n### Step 7: Verify Traces Are Being Collected\n\nCheck that traces are appearing in your observability backend:\n\n- **OTLP**: Check your OTLP receiver/collector logs for incoming traces\n- **Jaeger**: Navigate to the Jaeger UI and look for \"flipt\" service in the service list\n- **Zipkin**: Check your Zipkin UI for traces from the flipt service\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\nThere are no breaking changes in this release. All existing configurations remain valid and functional.\n\n## Bug Fixes\n\n- Fixed tracing tests to work with updated configuration structure\n- Improved error handling for invalid propagator configurations\n- Enhanced validation of sampling ratio values (must be between 0 and 1)\n\n## API Changes\n\n### No gRPC/REST API Changes\n\nThe gRPC and REST APIs remain unchanged. All existing clients and integrations will continue to work without modifications.\n\n### Configuration API Changes\n\nNew configuration schema additions:\n\n**New Fields in `tracing` section:**\n- `samplingRatio: number` (0-1, default: 1)\n- `propagators: array[string]` (valid values listed above, default: [\"tracecontext\", \"baggage\"])\n\nAll fields are optional and backward compatible.\n\n## Migration Path for Jaeger Users\n\nIf you're currently using the deprecated Jaeger exporter, follow these steps:\n\n1. **Option A: Migrate to OTLP with Jaeger Receiver**\n   - Deploy an OpenTelemetry Collector with Jaeger receiver\n   - Configure Flipt to send traces to the collector via OTLP\n   - Collector forwards traces to your Jaeger backend\n\n2. **Option B: Use Jaeger's OTLP Receiver**\n   - Enable OTLP receiver in your Jaeger configuration\n   - Update Flipt config to use OTLP exporter pointing to Jaeger\n   - Requires Jaeger v1.35+\n\n3. **Option C: Migrate to Alternative Backend**\n   - Move traces to a modern observability platform (Datadog, New Relic, etc.)\n   - Leverage Flipt's feature flag semantic conventions support\n\n## Known Issues\n\nNone at this time.\n\n## Testing Recommendations\n\nWhen upgrading, test the following scenarios:\n\n1. **Trace Collection**: Verify traces appear in your observability backend\n2. **Sampling**: Confirm that the sampling ratio is reducing trace volume as expected\n3. **Propagation**: For distributed systems, verify trace context is propagated between services\n4. **Performance**: Monitor Flipt's CPU and memory usage to ensure tracing overhead is acceptable\n5. **Feature Evaluations**: Ensure feature flag evaluations are still accurate and that trace attributes are correct\n\n## Resources\n\n- [OpenTelemetry Feature Flags Semantic Conventions](https://opentelemetry.io/docs/specs/semconv/feature-flags/feature-flags-spans/)\n- [OpenTelemetry Protocol (OTLP)](https://opentelemetry.io/docs/specs/otel/protocol/)\n- [Flipt Tracing Configuration Documentation](https://docs.flipt.io/configuration/tracing)\n- [OpenTelemetry Collector](https://opentelemetry.io/docs/collector/)\n\n## Questions or Issues?\n\nIf you encounter any issues with tracing configuration or have questions about the new features, please:\n\n1. The changes introduce better sampling control, distributed tracing propagator configuration, enhanced resource attributes, and support for OpenTelemetry Semantic Conventions for Feature Flags.\n\n## New Features\n\n### Tracing Configuration Enhancements\n\n#### **Sampling Ratio Control**\n- **Component**: [Tracing Configuration]\n- **Description**: Added `samplingRatio` configuration option to control the sampling rate of traces.\n- **Details**: The sampling ratio accepts a float value between 0 and 1 (inclusive), where:\n  - `0` = no traces are sampled (sampling disabled)\n  - `1` = all traces are sampled (no sampling)\n  - `0.1` = 10% of traces are sampled\n- **Configuration Example**:\n  ```yaml\n  tracing:\n    enabled: true\n    exporter: otlp\n    samplingRatio: 0.1  # Sample 10% of traces\n    otlp:\n      endpoint: localhost:4317\n  ```\n- **Default**: `1.0` (all traces sampled)\n- **API Reference**: Configuration is set via `flipt.schema.json` or YAML config files under `tracing.samplingRatio`\n\n#### **Multiple Propagator Support**\n- **Component**: [Tracing Configuration]\n- **Description**: Added support for configurable OpenTelemetry text map propagators to handle trace context propagation across services.\n- **Details**: Multiple propagators can be specified to support different distributed tracing standards. Supported options include:\n  - `tracecontext` — W3C Trace Context (default)\n  - `baggage` — W3C Baggage (default)\n  - `b3` — Zipkin B3 Single propagator\n  - `b3multi` — Zipkin B3 Multi propagator\n  - `jaeger` — Jaeger propagator\n  - `xray` — AWS X-Ray propagator\n  - `ottrace` — OT Trace propagator\n  - `none` — No propagation\n- **Configuration Example**:\n  ```yaml\n  tracing:\n    enabled: true\n    exporter: otlp\n    propagators:\n      - tracecontext\n      - baggage\n      - b3multi\n    otlp:\n      endpoint: localhost:4317\n  ```\n- **Default**: `[\"tracecontext\", \"baggage\"]`\n- **API Reference**: Configuration is set via `flipt.schema.json` or YAML config files under `tracing.propagators`\n\n### Enhanced Tracing Resource Attributes\n\n- **Component**: [OpenTelemetry Tracing]\n- **Description**: Improved the trace resource to include more comprehensive metadata about the Flipt service.\n- **Details**: The tracer provider now includes:\n  - Service name: `flipt`\n  - Service version: Flipt version\n  - Container information (if running in container)\n  - Host information (hostname, OS details)\n  - Process runtime information (Go version, runtime name)\n  - OTEL environment variables (automatic detection)\n  - Telemetry SDK information\n  - Schema URL for semantic convention compliance\n- **Impact**: Better trace correlation and service identification in distributed tracing backends\n\n### OpenTelemetry Semantic Conventions for Feature Flags\n\n- **Component**: [OTEL Attributes]\n- **Description**: Added support for OpenTelemetry's official semantic conventions for feature flags in span attributes.\n- **Details**: Trace spans now include standardized feature flag attributes:\n  - `ff.key` — The feature flag key (standardized attribute)\n  - `ff.provider_name` — The provider name set to \"Flipt\"\n  - `ff.variant` — The evaluated variant key (if applicable)\n  - Custom Flipt attributes:\n    - `flipt.flag` — Flag key\n    - `flipt.match` — Whether the flag matched\n    - `flipt.namespace` — Namespace key\n    - `flipt.flag_enabled` — Boolean flag enabled state\n    - `flipt.segment` — Segment key (deprecated)\n    - `flipt.segments` — List of matching segment keys\n    - `flipt.reason` — Evaluation reason\n    - `flipt.value` — Variant value\n    - `flipt.entity_id` — Entity ID\n    - `flipt.request_id` — Request ID\n- **Specification**: Follows [OpenTelemetry Feature Flags Semantic Conventions](https://opentelemetry.io/docs/specs/semconv/feature-flags/feature-flags-spans/)\n- **Impact**: Enables better trace analysis in observability platforms that support feature flag semantic conventions\n\n### OTEL Semantic Conventions Version Upgrade\n\n- **Component**: [OpenTelemetry Dependencies]\n- **Description**: Updated to the latest OpenTelemetry semantic conventions version (v1.24.0).\n- **Impact**: Access to latest semantic conventions and improved compatibility with modern observability backends\n\n## Configuration Examples\n\n### Basic OTLP Configuration with Sampling\n\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  samplingRatio: 0.5  # Sample 50% of traces\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: localhost:4317\n```\n\n### Advanced Configuration with Multiple Propagators\n\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  samplingRatio: 0.1\n  propagators:\n    - tracecontext\n    - baggage\n    - b3multi\n    - xray\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: otel-collector:4317\n    headers:\n      Authorization: Bearer your_token\n```\n\n### Jaeger Configuration with Sampling (Deprecated Exporter)\n\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: jaeger  # Deprecated - consider migrating to OTLP\n  samplingRatio: 1.0\n  jaeger:\n    host: localhost\n    port: 6831\n```\n\n### Zipkin Configuration with Propagators\n\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: zipkin\n  samplingRatio: 0.25\n  propagators:\n    - tracecontext\n    - baggage\n    - b3\n  zipkin:\n    endpoint: http://localhost:9411/api/v2/spans\n```\n\n## Deprecations\n\n### Jaeger Tracing Exporter (Existing Deprecation)\n\n- **Status**: Deprecated (as of v1.36.0)\n- **Details**: The Jaeger exporter is no longer actively maintained in OpenTelemetry. OpenTelemetry recommends using OTLP (OpenTelemetry Protocol) instead.\n- **Migration Path**:\n  1. Update your configuration to use `exporter: otlp`\n  2. Point to your Jaeger instance's OTLP receiver or use an OTLP-compatible backend\n  3. Test trace collection with the new configuration\n- **Timeline**: The Jaeger exporter will be removed in a future major version\n\n## Upgrade Guide\n\n### Step 1: Update Flipt\n\nUpdate to the latest version that includes these tracing improvements. The changes are backward compatible with existing configurations.\n\n### Step 2: Review Current Tracing Configuration (Optional)\n\nIf you are currently using tracing, check your existing configuration:\n\n```bash\n# Verify your current tracing configuration\ncat /path/to/your/flipt/config.yml | grep -A 20 \"^tracing:\"\n```\n\n### Step 3: Add Sampling Configuration (Recommended)\n\nTo optimize trace collection and reduce overhead, consider adding a sampling ratio:\n\n**Before:**\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: localhost:4317\n```\n\n**After:**\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  enabled: true\n  exporter: otlp\n  samplingRatio: 0.1  # Adjust based on your needs\n  otlp:\n    endpoint: localhost:4317\n```\n\n### Step 4: Configure Propagators (If Using Distributed Tracing)\n\nIf you're using distributed tracing with multiple services, specify propagators to match your infrastructure:\n\n**For W3C-compliant systems:**\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  propagators:\n    - tracecontext\n    - baggage\n```\n\n**For Zipkin-based systems:**\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  propagators:\n    - tracecontext\n    - baggage\n    - b3\n```\n\n**For AWS environments:**\n```yaml\ntracing:\n  propagators:\n    - tracecontext\n    - baggage\n    - xray\n```\n\n### Step 5: Validate Configuration\n\nTest your updated configuration:\n\n```bash\nflipt validate /path/to/your/flipt/config.yml\n```\n\nIf validation fails with propagator errors, check that all propagator names are valid (see list under \"Multiple Propagator Support\" above).\n\n### Step 6: Restart Flipt\n\nRestart your Flipt instance to apply the new configuration:\n\n```bash\n# Docker\ndocker restart flipt\n\n# Systemd\nsystemctl restart flipt\n\n# Manual\npkill flipt\n/path/to/flipt &\n```\n\n### Step 7: Verify Traces Are Being Collected\n\nCheck that traces are appearing in your observability backend:\n\n- **OTLP**: Check your OTLP receiver/collector logs for incoming traces\n- **Jaeger**: Navigate to the Jaeger UI and look for \"flipt\" service in the service list\n- **Zipkin**: Check your Zipkin UI for traces from the flipt service\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\nThere are no breaking changes in this release. All existing configurations remain valid and functional.\n\n## Bug Fixes\n\n- Fixed tracing tests to work with updated configuration structure\n- Improved error handling for invalid propagator configurations\n- Enhanced validation of sampling ratio values (must be between 0 and 1)\n\n## API Changes\n\n### No gRPC/REST API Changes\n\nThe gRPC and REST APIs remain unchanged. All existing clients and integrations will continue to work without modifications.\n\n### Configuration API Changes\n\nNew configuration schema additions:\n\n**New Fields in `tracing` section:**\n- `samplingRatio: number` (0-1, default: 1)\n- `propagators: array[string]` (valid values listed above, default: [\"tracecontext\", \"baggage\"])\n\nAll fields are optional and backward compatible.\n\n## Migration Path for Jaeger Users\n\nIf you're currently using the deprecated Jaeger exporter, follow these steps:\n\n1. **Option A: Migrate to OTLP with Jaeger Receiver**\n   - Deploy an OpenTelemetry Collector with Jaeger receiver\n   - Configure Flipt to send traces to the collector via OTLP\n   - Collector forwards traces to your Jaeger backend\n\n2. **Option B: Use Jaeger's OTLP Receiver**\n   - Enable OTLP receiver in your Jaeger configuration\n   - Update Flipt config to use OTLP exporter pointing to Jaeger\n   - Requires Jaeger v1.35+\n\n3. **Option C: Migrate to Alternative Backend**\n   - Move traces to a modern observability platform (Datadog, New Relic, etc.)\n   - Leverage Flipt's feature flag semantic conventions support\n\n## Known Issues\n\nNone at this time.\n\n## Testing Recommendations\n\nWhen upgrading, test the following scenarios:\n\n1. **Trace Collection**: Verify traces appear in your observability backend\n2. **Sampling**: Confirm that the sampling ratio is reducing trace volume as expected\n3. **Propagation**: For distributed systems, verify trace context is propagated between services\n4. **Performance**: Monitor Flipt's CPU and memory usage to ensure tracing overhead is acceptable\n5. **Feature Evaluations**: Ensure feature flag evaluations are still accurate and that trace attributes are correct\n\n## Resources\n\n- [OpenTelemetry Feature Flags Semantic Conventions](https://opentelemetry.io/docs/specs/semconv/feature-flags/feature-flags-spans/)\n- [OpenTelemetry Protocol (OTLP)](https://opentelemetry.io/docs/specs/otel/protocol/)\n- [Flipt Tracing Configuration Documentation](https://docs.flipt.io/configuration/tracing)\n- [OpenTelemetry Collector](https://opentelemetry.io/docs/collector/)\n\n## Questions or Issues?\n\nIf you encounter any issues with tracing configuration or have questions about the new features, please:\n\n1. Check the [Flipt Documentation](https://docs.flipt.io/)\n2. Review [Existing Issues on GitHub](https://github.com/flipt-io/flipt/issues)\n3. Open a [New Issue](https://github.com/flipt-io/flipt/issues/new) with details about your configuration and the problem\n4.
